# minimal_matmul WH grid sweep — all shapes, ascending util

Dense geometric M/K/N grid (32..8192), default auto path (heuristic on). util = tile-MAC throughput / observed peak (1239 tile-MAC/us). **orient**: N=normal(M<=N), T=transpose(M>N). **S**=N/M-slice (num_slices), **Pk**=K-split (num_k_slices); S1/Pk1 = no slicing/no K-par. PCC vs ttnn.matmul for every K-par shape, vs torch for small shapes (blank = skipped, plain large path).

WH 8x8. shapes=2816 (0 failures). K-par engaged=563 (20%). PCC-checked=1777 (K-par unverified=0), bad_pcc=0.
